<file path="ui/src/lib/components/views/OrthogonalView.test.ts">
import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach, afterEach } from 'vitest';
import { render, cleanup } from '@testing-library/svelte';
import { crosshairSlice } from '$lib/stores/crosshairSlice';
import OrthogonalView from './OrthogonalView.svelte';
import { ViewType } from '$lib/types/ViewType';

// Mock ResizeObserver
global.ResizeObserver = vi.fn().mockImplementation(() => ({
	observe: vi.fn(),
	disconnect: vi.fn(),
	unobserve: vi.fn()
}));

// Mock canvas getContext
HTMLCanvasElement.prototype.getContext = vi.fn().mockReturnValue({
	putImageData: vi.fn()
});

// Mock ImageData
global.ImageData = vi.fn().mockImplementation((data, width, height) => ({
	data,
	width,
	height
}));

// Mock the API
vi.mock('$lib/api', () => ({
	coreApi: {
		create_offscreen_render_target: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
		update_frame_ubo: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
		set_view_plane: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
		add_render_layer: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(undefined),
		render_to_image: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue('data:image/raw-rgba;base64,'),
	}
}));

// Mock the layer store
vi.mock('$lib/stores/layerStore', () => ({
	useLayerStore: {
		getState: () => ({
			layers: [
				{
					spec: {
						Volume: {
							id: 'test-layer-1'
						}
					},
					gpu: {
						atlas_layer_index: 0,
						texture_coords: {
							u_min: 0,
							v_min: 0,
							u_max: 1,
							v_max: 1
						}
					}
				}
			]
		})
	}
}));

describe('OrthogonalView - Dynamic Slice Updates', () => {
	let updateFrameUboSpy: any;
	
	beforeEach(async () => {
		// Reset crosshair to default state
		crosshairSlice.setState({
			crosshairWorldCoord: [0, 0, 0],
			activeViewPlane: 0
		});
		
		// Get spy for update_frame_ubo
		const { coreApi } = await import('$lib/api');
		updateFrameUboSpy = vi.mocked(coreApi).update_frame_ubo;
		updateFrameUboSpy.mockClear();
	});
	
	afterEach(() => {
		cleanup();
		vi.clearAllMocks();
	});
	
	it('should update rendering when crosshair position changes', async () => {
		// Render the component
		const { container } = render(OrthogonalView, {
			props: {
				layerId: 'test-layer-1',
				viewType: ViewType.Axial
			}
		});
		
		// Wait for initial render
		await vi.waitFor(() => {
			expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		});
		
		// Clear the spy to track only new calls
		updateFrameUboSpy.mockClear();
		
		// Change crosshair position
		crosshairSlice.setState({
			crosshairWorldCoord: [10, 20, 30],
			activeViewPlane: 0
		});
		
		// Wait for the effect to trigger
		await vi.waitFor(() => {
			expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		});
		
		// Verify the update was called with new crosshair position
		const lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
		const crosshairVoxel = lastCall[2]; // Third argument is crosshairVoxel
		
		expect(crosshairVoxel).toEqual([10, 20, 30, 1]);
	});
	
	it('should update correct slice based on view type', async () => {
		// Set crosshair position before rendering
		crosshairSlice.setState({
			crosshairWorldCoord: [50, 60, 70],
			activeViewPlane: 0
		});
		
		// Test Axial view
		const { rerender } = render(OrthogonalView, {
			props: {
				layerId: 'test-layer-1',
				viewType: ViewType.Axial
			}
		});
		
		// Wait for initial render
		await vi.waitFor(() => {
			expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		});
		
		// Check view plane distance for Axial (Z coordinate)
		let lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
		let viewPlaneDistance = lastCall[4]; // Fifth argument
		expect(viewPlaneDistance).toBe(70); // Z coordinate for Axial
		
		// Test Coronal view
		updateFrameUboSpy.mockClear();
		await rerender({
			layerId: 'test-layer-1',
			viewType: ViewType.Coronal
		});
		
		// Wait a bit for render
		await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
		
		// The rerender should trigger setupViewRenderParams again
		expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
		viewPlaneDistance = lastCall[4];
		expect(viewPlaneDistance).toBe(60); // Y coordinate for Coronal
		
		// Test Sagittal view
		updateFrameUboSpy.mockClear();
		await rerender({
			layerId: 'test-layer-1',
			viewType: ViewType.Sagittal
		});
		
		// Wait a bit for render
		await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
		
		expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
		viewPlaneDistance = lastCall[4];
		expect(viewPlaneDistance).toBe(50); // X coordinate for Sagittal
	});
	
	it('should not update when crosshair is null', async () => {
		// Set crosshair to null
		crosshairSlice.setState({
			crosshairWorldCoord: null,
			activeViewPlane: 0
		});
		
		// Render the component
		render(OrthogonalView, {
			props: {
				layerId: 'test-layer-1',
				viewType: ViewType.Axial
			}
		});
		
		// Wait a bit
		await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
		
		// Initial setup might be called, but check that it uses default [0,0,0]
		if (updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length > 0) {
			const lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
			const crosshairVoxel = lastCall[2];
			expect(crosshairVoxel).toEqual([0, 0, 0, 1]); // Default position
		}
	});
	
	it('should handle rapid crosshair changes', async () => {
		// Render the component
		render(OrthogonalView, {
			props: {
				layerId: 'test-layer-1',
				viewType: ViewType.Axial
			}
		});
		
		// Wait for initial render
		await vi.waitFor(() => {
			expect(updateFrameUboSpy).toHaveBeenCalled();
		});
		
		const initialCallCount = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length;
		
		// Rapidly change crosshair position
		for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
			crosshairSlice.setState({
				crosshairWorldCoord: [i * 10, i * 20, i * 30],
				activeViewPlane: 0
			});
			// Small delay between changes
			await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 10));
		}
		
		// Wait for effects to settle
		await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
		
		// Should have received multiple updates
		expect(updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length).toBeGreaterThan(initialCallCount);
		
		// Check the last update has the final position
		const lastCall = updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls[updateFrameUboSpy.mock.calls.length - 1];
		const crosshairVoxel = lastCall[2];
		expect(crosshairVoxel).toEqual([40, 80, 120, 1]); // Final position
	});
});

describe('OrthogonalView - Crosshair Click Updates', () => {
	it('should update crosshair when clicking on the canvas', async () => {
		// TODO: Implement click-to-set-crosshair functionality
		// This test is a placeholder for future implementation
		expect(true).toBe(true);
	});
});

<file path="ui/src/lib/components/views/OrthogonalViewContainer.svelte">
<script lang="ts">
	/**
	 * @component OrthogonalViewContainer
	 * @description Container for managing three orthogonal views with shared GPU context
	 */
	import { onMount, onDestroy } from 'svelte';
	import { coreApi } from '$lib/api';
	import { useLayerStore } from '$lib/stores/layerStore';
	import { crosshairSlice } from '$lib/stores/crosshairSlice';
	import { ViewType } from '$lib/types/ViewType';
	import OrthogonalViewGPU from './OrthogonalViewGPU.svelte';

	// Props
	let {
		selectedLayerId
	}: {
		selectedLayerId: string | null;
	} = $props();

	// State
	let gpuInitialized = $state(false);
	let initError = $state<string | null>(null);
	let viewports = $state({
		[ViewType.Axial]: { scale: 1.0, offset: [0, 0] as [number, number] },
		[ViewType.Coronal]: { scale: 1.0, offset: [0, 0] as [number, number] },
		[ViewType.Sagittal]: { scale: 1.0, offset: [0, 0] as [number, number] }
	});

	// Initialize GPU context once for all views
	async function initializeGPUContext() {
		try {
			console.log('OrthogonalViewContainer: Checking GPU context...');
			// init_render_loop is idempotent, but let's not call it multiple times
			gpuInitialized = true;
			console.log('OrthogonalViewContainer: GPU context ready');
		} catch (err) {
			console.error('Failed to initialize GPU context:', err);
			initError = `Failed to initialize GPU: ${err}`;
		}
	}

	// Handle viewport changes from individual views
	function handleViewportChange(viewType: ViewType, viewport: { scale: number; offset: [number, number] }) {
		viewports[viewType] = viewport;
	}

	// Handle crosshair click in a view
	function handleCrosshairClick(viewType: ViewType, position: { x: number; y: number }) {
		// Convert 2D click position to 3D voxel coordinates based on view type
		const currentCrosshair = crosshairSlice.getState();
		
		switch (viewType) {
			case ViewType.Axial:
				// Click on axial view updates X and Y
				crosshairSlice.setState({
					x: Math.round(position.x),
					y: Math.round(position.y),
					z: currentCrosshair.z
				});
				break;
			case ViewType.Coronal:
				// Click on coronal view updates X and Z
				crosshairSlice.setState({
					x: Math.round(position.x),
					y: currentCrosshair.y,
					z: Math.round(position.y)
				});
				break;
			case ViewType.Sagittal:
				// Click on sagittal view updates Y and Z
				crosshairSlice.setState({
					x: currentCrosshair.x,
					y: Math.round(position.x),
					z: Math.round(position.y)
				});
				break;
		}
	}

	// Synchronize view scales (optional feature)
	let syncViewScales = $state(true);
	
	$effect(() => {
		if (syncViewScales) {
			// When one view scale changes, update all views to match
			const maxScale = Math.max(
				viewports[ViewType.Axial].scale,
				viewports[ViewType.Coronal].scale,
				viewports[ViewType.Sagittal].scale
			);
			
			if (viewports[ViewType.Axial].scale !== maxScale ||
				viewports[ViewType.Coronal].scale !== maxScale ||
				viewports[ViewType.Sagittal].scale !== maxScale) {
				
				viewports = {
					[ViewType.Axial]: { ...viewports[ViewType.Axial], scale: maxScale },
					[ViewType.Coronal]: { ...viewports[ViewType.Coronal], scale: maxScale },
					[ViewType.Sagittal]: { ...viewports[ViewType.Sagittal], scale: maxScale }
				};
			}
		}
	});

	onMount(() => {
		console.log('OrthogonalViewContainer mounted');
		initializeGPUContext();
	});

	onDestroy(() => {
		// Cleanup is handled by individual views
	});
</script>

<div class="orthogonal-view-container">
	{#if initError}
		<div class="init-error">
			<h3>GPU Initialization Error</h3>
			<p>{initError}</p>
		</div>
	{:else if !gpuInitialized}
		<div class="init-loading">
			<p>Initializing GPU context...</p>
		</div>
	{:else}
		<div class="view-grid">
			<div class="view-panel axial">
				<OrthogonalViewGPU
					layerId={selectedLayerId}
					viewType={ViewType.Axial}
					onViewportChange={handleViewportChange}
				/>
			</div>
			
			<div class="view-panel coronal">
				<OrthogonalViewGPU
					layerId={selectedLayerId}
					viewType={ViewType.Coronal}
					onViewportChange={handleViewportChange}
				/>
			</div>
			
			<div class="view-panel sagittal">
				<OrthogonalViewGPU
					layerId={selectedLayerId}
					viewType={ViewType.Sagittal}
					onViewportChange={handleViewportChange}
				/>
			</div>
		</div>
		
		<div class="view-controls">
			<label>
				<input type="checkbox" bind:checked={syncViewScales} />
				Synchronize view scales
			</label>
		</div>
	{/if}
</div>

<style>
	.orthogonal-view-container {
		width: 100%;
		height: 100%;
		display: flex;
		flex-direction: column;
